{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2021-04-08 01:38:07","updatedTime":"2021-04-08 01:38:07","title":"What Is a Breakout Session? [+ How To Plan Your Own]","link":"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/breakout-session","description":"<p>Having gone to many meetings, I can definitely say that I sometimes get overwhelmed. While I enjoy the content being discussed, I can feel tired and wish for a break to decompress before throwing my mind back into absorbing the information.</p> \n<p>I’m sure I’m not alone in these feelings, that many of us want to absorb all we can while still having the opportunity to temporarily disconnect and let our minds wander.</p> \n<p>What we’re looking for is a breakout session, where meeting hosts understand and accommodate for the need to take a break and specifically carve out time for them. This post will explain what a breakout session is, explain how to plan for a successful one, and present ideas that you can incorporate into your next meeting.</p> \n<p><a class=\"cta_button\" href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/cs/ci/?pg=7ad084e3-bb2d-429e-9cbd-2b09416729f1&amp;pid=53&amp;ecid=&amp;hseid=&amp;hsic=\"><img class=\"hs-cta-img \" style=\"border-width: 0px; /*hs-extra-styles*/; margin: 0 auto; display: block; margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px\" alt=\"Download free resources for executing your best event yet. [Free Kit]\" src=\"https://no-cache.hubspot.com/cta/default/53/7ad084e3-bb2d-429e-9cbd-2b09416729f1.png\" align=\"middle\"></a></p> \n<p></p> \n<p>These sessions are less structured than general meeting sessions, and typically allow attendees to participate instead of simply sitting in the audience and listening. While these sessions can be related to the overall meeting content, they can also focus on unrelated topics.</p> \n<p>Breakout sessions can happen during both in-person and virtual meetings. The former typically send attendees to different areas of a conference venue, and the latter use breakout room functions native to virtual conferencing tools. These sessions are especially important during virtual meetings, where there is already an element of built-in disconnection as attendees are in their own respective locations.</p> \n<p>Below we’ll go over some ideas that you can use to incorporate engaging breakout sessions into your upcoming meetings.</p> \n<h2>Breakout Session Ideas</h2> \n<p>There are various breakout sessions you can plan for, like those directly related to meeting content and others that are entertainment-focused and involve attendees playing games with each other.</p> \n<h3>Lightning Talks</h3> \n<p>Lightning talks are a great way to break up meeting sessions. They’re short so people can attend more than one, and a facilitator takes a set amount of time to give brief talks on a subject of their choice related to overall meeting content.</p> \n<p>However, lightning talks can also be adapted to allow facilitators to present on any topic they’re passionate about, helping attendees get to know more about each other and let their minds drift elsewhere before re-focusing on meetings.</p> \n<h3>Speed Networking</h3> \n<p>Speed networking breakout sessions allow attendees to meet each other and establish professional connections. You can divide people up, set expectations, and instruct participants to spend a set amount of time talking to one person and moving on to another once the time is up.</p> \n<h3>Games</h3> \n<p>Games can help participants let loose and de-stress, especially when they’re interactive and encourage engagement with others. These sessions are different from the other ideas on this list as they can be less related to meeting content than others.</p> \n<p>During in-person sessions, you can organize bingo games, team people up to solve puzzles, or even play charades. <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/online-team-building-games?_ga=2.258830282.1142681397.1616188169-1118502603.1616188169\">Virtual games</a>&nbsp;are possible as well.</p> \n<h3>Goal-setting Sessions</h3> \n<p>Goal-setting sessions are great as they can encourage participants to think in-depth about meeting content in a relaxed setting where they can have conversations with others and express their thoughts. You can assign a facilitator to each breakout room, and they can initiate a conversation about general meeting content and encourage participants to relate the content to their desires.</p> \n<p>For example, suppose your larger meeting is focused on introducing a new business-wide workflow. In that case, attendees in these sessions can set goals surrounding what they want to accomplish with the new strategy over the next year.</p> \n<h3>Ask Me Anything (AMA) Sessions</h3> \n<p>AMA sessions are an excellent breakout idea, especially if you don’t have the chance to answer everyone's questions.</p> \n<p>Participants can be separated into different rooms and groups and ask questions or express their thoughts about what has happened during the meeting, and an experienced facilitator can be there to answer them.</p> \n<h3>Outdoor Activities</h3> \n<p>Outdoor activities are best suited for in-person meetings where groups of participants can go outside together. They can be less content-focused and involve something like a scavenger hunt, but general breakout sessions can also be held outdoors to give participants a change of scenery.</p> \n<p>However, making use of an outdoor session during a virtual meeting can involve encouraging participants to log off for a few minutes, go outside, and come back and tell the group about something they saw while they were out there, or to share a photo of an item you asked them to find and identify outside.</p> \n<h3>Open Mic Session</h3> \n<p>Open mics are always exciting, and they can be great for encouraging engagement and giving attendees a moment to have fun and learn about their peers. Open mics can center around meeting content, like having service representatives share customer stories, or unrelated and attendees stand up and share a hidden talent.</p> \n<h3>Drop-in Discussions</h3> \n<p>Drop-in discussions are a great idea as you can schedule multiple different sessions for attendees to choose from. They’re also a low-pressure format for engaging in conversation and networking. People can navigate to a room where the content is related to their interest, and even pop-in to multiple sessions if they can’t decide.</p> \n<p>While this is not an exhaustive list of ideas, they can certainly be used to create and design engaging breakout sessions for your next meeting.</p> \n<h2>Breakout Session Examples</h2> \n<p>Below we’ll go over some real-life examples of breakout sessions that can serve as additional inspiration for your planning.</p> \n<h3>Nonprofit Leadership Center</h3> \n<p>The Nonprofit Leadership Center is an organization that supports other nonprofits. It hosts a yearly leadership conference that includes multiple breakout sessions led by industry leaders that attendees can choose from.</p> \n<p>A Breakout session from their 2020 conference, <a href=\"https://nlctb.org/news/2020-leadership-conference-breakouts/\">Courageous Conversations: Understanding &amp; Confronting Unconscious Bias with Margarita Sarmiento</a>, discussed how to create work environments that were inclusive and positive for all to be part of. The breakout session related to the overarching theme of the conference, which focused on <a href=\"https://nlctb.org/events/2020-leadership-conference/\">leading courageously</a>.</p> \n<h3>Building On Our Momentum (BOOM)</h3> \n<p>Mount Holyoke College hosts an annual diversity conference called Building On Our Momentum, where community members are encouraged to attend events and learn about diversity, equity, and inclusion in live talks and recorded content.</p> \n<p>The <a href=\"https://events.mtholyoke.edu/boom_2021\">2021 BOOM conference</a>&nbsp;incorporates various breakout sessions to help attendees engage with content in smaller groups and decompress from hard-hitting topics that they may be learning about.</p> \n<p>One of the sessions, <a href=\"https://embark.mtholyoke.edu/osi/rsvp_boot?id=1054959\">Tuesday Crafternoon: Zines</a>, encourages attendees to get creative and create a zine while simultaneously learning about their history and use in marginalized communities.</p> \n<h3>INBOUND</h3> \n<p>INBOUND is HubSpot’s annual marketing conference that features a wide variety of opportunities, including breakout sessions. During these sessions, attendees can decompress, further engage with content, and connect with other participants.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://events.bizzabo.com/225435/agenda/session/328400\">Meetup: Black at INBOUND</a>, an INBOUND 2020 breakout session, created a safe space for Black attendees to meet other professionals, network, and discuss topics of interest.</p> \n<h2>Breakout Session Template</h2> \n<p>Given the benefits that they can provide, it’s essential to understand how to plan for, and lead, a successful breakout session. Let’s go over some tips.</p> \n<h3>1. Set designated time frames.</h3> \n<p>As breakout sessions are specific periods between main meeting sessions, it’s crucial to set specific time frames in which they will occur. Take note of the session’s activity, how long it will take, and aim to stick to that schedule.</p> \n<h3>2. Set session goals.</h3> \n<p>Breakout sessions that are specifically designed for attendees to decompress are great, but, regardless of intention, it’s essential to set goals, so participants know what to expect.</p> \n<p>Maybe it’s simply just to network and make conversation, but it could also be to outline personal goals. Letting people know what to expect helps you ensure that these sessions stay focused and attendees can accomplish everything within the desired time frame.</p> \n<h3>3. Design seating to complement the breakout format.</h3> \n<p>This tip is more related to in-person sessions, but essential nonetheless. It’s important to create seating arrangements and set up meeting spaces that complement and facilitate the session intent.</p> \n<p>For example, a room filled with round tables wouldn’t be conducive to a speed networking session where two people are in discussion with each other. Understand what you want participants to accomplish during the decision, and design a meeting space accordingly.</p> \n<h3>4. Use the correct equipment.</h3> \n<p>Using the right equipment is relevant to both in-person and virtual breakout sessions, as you’ll want to ensure you have everything you need ahead of time. For example, suppose you’re leading a breakout session game. In that case, you want to make sure that you have all the necessary materials to run the session smoothly, like enough pieces for all participants and printable instructions to refer to during the game.</p> \n<p>Having the right equipment is also important because these sessions are meant to help people decompress, so you don’t want to leave people waiting or stressed about what is about to happen, especially during virtual events.</p> \n<p>All in all, breakout sessions are valuable aspects of meetings, both virtual and in-person. They give attendees a chance to connect with other participants, think deeply about meeting content, and generally have fun and engaging conversations.</p> \n<p>Leverage the tips on this list when planning for your next meeting, and you’ll likely receive feedback from attendees that the sessions were engaging, exciting, and have inspired them to attend your next event.</p> \n<p></p> \n<p><a class=\"cta_button\" href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/cs/ci/?pg=bd0c27ef-31a6-464a-b8a8-a65cbc33e2a5&amp;pid=53&amp;ecid=&amp;hseid=&amp;hsic=\"><img class=\"hs-cta-img \" style=\"border-width: 0px; /*hs-extra-styles*/; \" alt=\"Free Resource: How to Reach &amp; Engage Your Audience on Facebook\" src=\"https://no-cache.hubspot.com/cta/default/53/9f7c45b7-c71b-4797-8d5d-e6b296fb6a83.png\"></a></p> \n<p>So, how do you gain followers? We know buying them doesn't work because it rarely translates to engagement. The good news is that there are at least 20 ways to gain them organically.</p> \n<p>Let's cover them below.</p> \n<h2 style=\"font-weight: bold;\">1. Develop your Facebook marketing strategy.</h2> \n<p>Having a <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/social-media-strategy-for-your-business?_ga=2.62409388.1481247633.1616124450-1598130191.1616124450\">social media strategy</a> for your Facebook Business Page is the first step in attracting followers to your brand. A robust strategy gives your team direction and a playbook from which to develop new ideas. It also helps you assess your performance from the right lens.</p> \n<p>When developing your playbook, here are a few questions to consider:</p> \n<ul> \n <li>What does success look like?</li> \n <li>What does our audience want to see?</li> \n <li>How should we engage our audience?</li> \n <li>What tactics are our competitors using on Facebook?</li> \n</ul> \n<p>Once you are clear on your approach, it will be easier to explore the growth methods outlined below.</p> \n<h2>2. Post often.</h2> \n<p><a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/how-frequently-should-i-publish-on-social-media\">Your posting schedule</a> is undoubtedly linked to your followers. Why? The more you post, the more visible you are to your target audience and the more likely you are to reach new users.</p> \n<p>Here are two tools to streamline your publishing process:</p> \n<ul> \n <li><strong><a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/social-media-calendar-tools\">A content calendar</a></strong> – This is used to plan out what content you will post to your social media platforms and when they will be published. It's especially helpful to have a content calendar to align your social media content with upcoming events, such as product or service launches.</li> \n <li><strong>A social media publishing tool </strong>– Manually publishing to your Facebook Page can be time-consuming and take you away from more important tasks. With a publishing tool, you can schedule your posts to go live at a specific time and date, and have the peace of mind that your page will always be active.</li> \n</ul> \n<h2>3. Host giveaways.</h2> \n<p>Giveaways can be an effective and low-cost way to build brand awareness and attract new Facebook users to your Facebook Page.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/facebook-giveaway\">To maximize the impact of your giveaway</a>, set rules that encourage audience participation. For instance, your giveaway can require each user to tag a friend in the giveaway post and make a post of their own to qualify to win.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/get-more-followers-example-png.png?width=600&amp;name=get-more-followers-example-png.png\" width=\"600\" style=\"width: 600px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\" alt=\"Facebook Giveaway Example \"></p> \n<p style=\"font-size: 12px; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"https://www.facebook.com/OREOUnitedStates/photos/a.597325737403442/995804524222226/\">Image Source</a></p> \n<p>The more engagement you can get from your followers, the better chance your giveaway will reach new users.</p> \n<h2>4. Vary your posts.</h2> \n<p>One of the reasons why your follower count may have plateaued is because your content isn't connecting with consumers.</p> \n<p>Start experimenting with various types of posts to see what garners more shares, comments, and other forms of engagement. You may find that videos perform much better than images, or that covering certain topics get more shares than others.</p> \n<p>As you notice trends in what's working and what's not, tweak your strategy, observe, and keep experimenting.</p> \n<h2>5. Post at the right time.</h2> \n<p>If you post something on Facebook but no one's around to see it, does it make an impact?</p> \n<p>With social media, visibility is key. The first part of increasing your visibility is posting regularly, but you also have to align your posting schedule with your audience's scrolling habits.</p> \n<p>If your users are most active on Facebook between 5:00 and 9:00 PM., that's your time to publish your content. Publish outside of that window and you risk your content being missed altogether.</p> \n<h2>6. Create shareable content.</h2> \n<p>Whenever you see something that's informative, entertaining, inspiring, or just interesting, what's your first instinct nowadays? Mine is to hit the \"share\" button and send it to other people.</p> \n<p>Making shareable content is one of the best ways to get followers because it expands your reach.</p> \n<p>What makes something have that shareable quality? It varies, depending on the audience you're targeting, but one common thread is that it has to resonate. Maybe your content addresses a concern they have, or it discusses a topic they're interested in.</p> \n<p>This viral video from HubSpot garnered over 760K views and shows how to take a buzzy topic, like Game of Thrones, and apply it to your brand.</p> \n<iframe style=\"border: none; overflow: hidden; margin: 0px auto; display: block;\" src=\"https://www.facebook.com/plugins/video.php?height=314&amp;href=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.facebook.com%2Fhubspot%2Fvideos%2F10156165276484394%2F&amp;show_text=false&amp;width=560\" width=\"560\" height=\"314\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen></iframe> \n<p>Shareable content is also easy to digest – there's a reason why the most viral videos are typically from <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/brands-on-tiktok\">TikTok</a> and <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/instagram-reels-examples\">Instagram Reels</a>. They're short and get to the point.</p> \n<p>For instance, this 40-second video by <a href=\"http://asos.com\">ASOS</a> is weird, funny and has over 300K views.<span style=\"color: #33475b;\"></span></p> \n<iframe style=\"border: none; overflow: hidden; margin: 0px auto; display: block;\" src=\"https://www.facebook.com/plugins/video.php?height=476&amp;href=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.facebook.com%2Fasos.us%2Fvideos%2F848504299231734%2F&amp;show_text=true&amp;width=380\" width=\"380\" height=\"591\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen></iframe> \n<p>Lastly, make sure your content is visually appealing. If your team doesn't have the bandwidth to invest internal resources to create these creative assets, consider outsourcing them through independent contractors.</p> \n<h2>7. Interact with your audience.</h2> \n<p>Facebook users, like most social media users, like to feel seen and heard by the brands they engage with. Your brand should make it a priority to interact with your followers regularly, whether it's answering a direct message or responding to a comment under your latest post.</p> \n<p>These interactions not only boost your engagement rate but can also build brand loyalty. And we all know that a consumer who is loyal to a brand will spread the word and bring on more brand promoters, serving as unofficial influencers.</p> \n<h2>8. Promote your Facebook Page everywhere.</h2> \n<p>If your goal is to gain more followers on your business page, you should direct traffic to your page whenever possible. There are a few ways to do this:</p> \n<ul> \n <li>Add a Facebook plugin to your website.</li> \n <li>Include a CTA in your email newsletter to encourage your subscribers to visit your Facebook Page.</li> \n <li>Embed your Facebook posts whenever relevant in your blog posts.</li> \n <li>Host your giveaways only on Facebook.</li> \n <li>Promote your Facebook Page on other social media platforms.</li> \n</ul> \n<h2>9. Add your Facebook social link to all digital platforms.</h2> \n<p>Your Facebook link should be accessible everywhere you have an online presence. This includes your website, email, and social media platforms.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/passamaquoddy-maple-example-png.png?width=600&amp;name=passamaquoddy-maple-example-png.png\" width=\"600\" style=\"width: 600px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\" alt=\"&quot;Connect With Us&quot; brand example\"></p> \n<p style=\"font-size: 12px; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"https://www.passamaquoddymaple.com/\">Image Source</a></p> \n<p>It’s as simple as putting “Follow Us,” or “Connect With Us” with the social icons, as shown in the business above.</p> \n<p>The easier it is to find you, the better your chances of gaining followers.</p> \n<h2>10. Work with influencers.</h2> \n<p><a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/brand-influencer\">Working with influencers</a> is great for many reasons, the main one being the credibility they give to your brand. When an influencer promotes a brand, it's social proof (i.e., a stamp of approval).</p> \n<p>You can work with influencers to target an audience you haven't yet connected with and drive traffic to your Facebook Page.</p> \n<p>Beyond that, studies show consumers tend to trust the word of an influencer more than a brand's word. So, by collaborating with influencers, you can earn new followers who already have a certain level of trust in your brand.</p> \n<h2>11. Partner up with another brand.</h2> \n<p><a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/blog/tabid/6307/bid/34188/what-in-the-heck-is-co-marketing.aspx\">Co-marketing </a>is a collaboration between two brands with similar audiences and marketing goals who team up for marketing efforts.</p> \n<p>A co-marketing campaign on Facebook could look like a video series released over a month or week-long Facebook Live events hosted with your partner.</p> \n<p>This strategy allows brands to use their individual distribution channels to reach new people and share the results of the campaign.</p> \n<h2>12. Offer a coupon.</h2> \n<p>In addition to giveaways, there are other ways to incentivize your audience to promote your brand, including offering coupons.</p> \n<p>With a plugin like <a href=\"https://apps.shopify.com/facebook-likes-popup?prev_msid=e89616a0-A6EC-43F9-2D64-50F33B8CB26D\">Shopify's Facebook Likes Popup</a>, for example, you can offer a discount code to consumers who like your Facebook Page as they are completing a purchase on your site.</p> \n<p>You can also offer discount codes to encourage Facebook reviews, which serve as social proof and can help you gain more followers.</p> \n<h2>13. Join Facebook Groups.</h2> \n<p><a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/best-facebook-groups-examples\">Joining a Facebook Group</a> can give you direct access to your target audience.</p> \n<p>You can get direct insight into your audience's needs, concerns, likes, and dislikes. In addition, it's another channel to connect with them more intimately.</p> \n<p>But keep in mind, it's not a place for selling – use it as a way to introduce yourself to your target personas and build authentic connections.</p> \n<h2>14. Create your own Facebook Group.</h2> \n<p><a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/create-facebook-group\">Having your own Facebook Group </a>is arguably the second-best channel you can have behind an email list.</p> \n<p>Similar to email subscribers, a Facebook Group user has opted to join your group and stays in because it adds value to their lives.</p> \n<p>It's another way to attract your target audience, build a strong community, and provide value to your user personas.</p> \n<h2>15. Learn from your Facebook Insights dashboard.</h2> \n<p><a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/facebook-insights\">Your Facebook Insights dashboard</a> is where your page's analytics live.</p> \n<p>It tells you how users are behaving on your Facebook Business Page and how your posts are performing.</p> \n<p>Use it as a resource to identify which strategies are earning you followers and what's worth changing.</p> \n<h2>16. Use hashtags in your posts.</h2> \n<p>Hashtags are a great discoverability tool on Facebook. You can use them to help your target market find your post and increase your follower count.</p> \n<p>It's important to use a mix of popular and niche hashtags to ensure that your posts are getting enough visibility without disappearing in a sea of posts.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/get-more-followers-example-1-png.png?width=453&amp;name=get-more-followers-example-1-png.png\" width=\"453\" style=\"width: 453px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\" alt=\"Example of how to use hashtags to get more followers\"></p> \n<p>For instance, <a href=\"http://powerchord.com\">PowerChord</a> used a mix of geo-specific hashtags to reach local Facebook users and topic-specific hashtags to reach audiences interested in the subject.</p> \n<h2>17. Make your page easier to find.</h2> \n<p>The last thing you want is someone who wants to follow your page but can't seem to find it. While some may be persistent, others may give up once their initial search is unsuccessful.</p> \n<p>To avoid this issue altogether, optimize your Facebook Page for search to ensure you'll always be easy to find. Here are some ways to do so:</p> \n<ul> \n <li>Use the same username on all your social media profiles.</li> \n <li>Add your logo to your profile picture and add a cover photo that reflects your brand.</li> \n <li>Have a complete \"About\" section.</li> \n <li>Keep your contact information and business hours updated.</li> \n</ul> \n<h2>18. Don't over-promote.</h2> \n<p>Your Facebook Page should be used to connect with your target audience and publish content that resonates with them.</p> \n<p>While a certain level of promotion is expected, it shouldn’t be the majority of what you post. Depending on your industry, pushing your products and services could repel your audience and lead to high unfollow rates.</p> \n<h2>19. Authenticate your page.</h2> \n<p>Social media is rampant with bots and fake business pages aiming to deceive consumers. This can make Facebook users a little reluctant to follow brands they don't recognize.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hubfs/facebook-verification-badge-png.png\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\" alt=\"Facebook verification badge example\"></p> \n<p>Authenticating your page can give your brand the credibility needed to both protect your audience against fraudulent pages and give them the reassurance they need. To request a verification badge on Facebook, you must fill out <a href=\"https://www.facebook.com/help/contact/342509036134712\">this form</a>.</p> \n<h2>20. Create original content.</h2> \n<p>As new social media platforms gain popularity, it's easy to recycle content from one platform to another. While that does make posting regularly easier, it may be hurting your engagement.</p> \n<p>Every social media platform is different and so are its users. For instance, Facebook users tend to prefer videos over other forms of content, <a href=\"https://buffer.com/resources/facebook-marketing-2019/\">according to a 2019 Buffer study</a>. The best performing content on Facebook is funny, entertaining, or practical.</p> \n<p>With this in mind, it's important to customize your content to the platform. <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/examples-repurposing-content\">Repurposing</a> can stretch the life of your content. However, it shouldn't be your only strategy. Be sure to listen to your audience and build content around their needs.</p> \n<h2>21. Run ads.</h2> \n<p>In addition to all the steps mentioned above, you can also <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/facebook-paid-ad-checklist\">run ads to reach more Facebook users. </a></p> \n<p>Facebook Ads allows you to target users based on demographics, behaviors, and interests. This guarantees that you reach users who match your user persona and are more likely to convert.</p> \n<p>Getting more followers on Facebook requires more than just posting regularly. You have to tap into what attracts your audience – through data analysis and community engagement – to develop sustainable strategies.</p> \n<p><a class=\"cta_button\" 01:38:07","updatedTime":"2021-04-08 01:38:07","title":"How 7 Brands Use Facebook Stories for Business","link":"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/examples-of-facebook-stories","description":"<p>Whenever a new feature comes out on social media, I am usually a late adopter.</p>  \n<p>Back when Instagram launched <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/instagram-stories?_ga=2.202129425.1220013014.1616181815-474576179.1616181815\">Stories</a>, a worthy <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/how-to-use-snapchat-for-business\">Snapchat</a> opponent, I thought, \"<em>Hm, I don't know about this</em>.\" Perhaps it's because change, even if slight, is uncomfortable or just because I'm naturally a cautious person.</p> \n<p><a class=\"cta_button\" href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/cs/ci/?pg=9f7c45b7-c71b-4797-8d5d-e6b296fb6a83&amp;pid=53&amp;ecid=&amp;hseid=&amp;hsic=\"><img class=\"hs-cta-img \" style=\"border-width: 0px; /*hs-extra-styles*/; \" alt=\"Free Resource: How to Reach &amp; Engage Your Audience on Facebook\" src=\"https://no-cache.hubspot.com/cta/default/53/9f7c45b7-c71b-4797-8d5d-e6b296fb6a83.png\"></a></p> \n<p>But here we are a few years after its launch and I barely look at my newsfeed. Where am I? You guessed it, endlessly swiping through Stories.</p> \n<p>The feature gained steam on Instagram but was then integrated on Facebook. Now, every brand with a <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/blog/tabid/6307/bid/24422/the-ultimate-facebook-marketing-cheat-sheet.aspx\">Facebook Business Page</a> has gained another marketing tool to reach users.</p> \n<p>So, what exactly can you post on Facebook Stories? Get inspired by these eight brands.</p> \n<h2>Examples of Facebook Stories for Business</h2> \n<h3>A Look Behind the Scenes</h3> \n<p>Back when Facebook only allowed brands to publish posts, brands were probably more selective about their content, knowing it would stay there permanently.</p> \n<p>Now that Facebook Stories is here, brands can have a little bit more fun with what they post knowing the content will only be available for the next 24 hours.</p> \n<p>That's why behind-the-scenes content is perfect for Facebook Stories. It's not necessarily important enough to be featured on the news feed but it can be a great way to create some buzz around an upcoming release.<img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/facebook-story-example-woven-nook-jpg.jpeg?width=274&amp;name=facebook-story-example-woven-nook-jpg.jpeg\" style=\"font-style: normal; font-variant-ligatures: normal; font-variant-caps: normal; font-weight: 400; font-size: 18px; font-family: AvenirNext, 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, Arial, sans-serif; width: 274px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\" width=\"274\" alt=\"Woven Nook Facebook Story Example\">In this example, <a href=\"http://wovennook.com\">Woven Nook</a>, a home decor company, posts a Story to tease an upcoming project. The Story allows the brand to create some anticipation around the project and also gauge the audience's interest in this type of content.</p> \n<p>Another important element in this Story is that it features one of the founders of the company. In recent years, <a href=\"https://sproutsocial.com/insights/data/social-media-connection/\">studies have shown </a>that consumers connect more with brands who pull back the curtains and show the faces behind the business.</p> \n<p>Woven Nook could have posted the sneak peek without the founder. However, having a human featured in the image can leave a stronger impression than just a setting.</p> \n<h3>Polls and Surveys</h3> \n<p>Facebook Stories isn't just another publishing channel, it also has great features that help brands connect with and engage their audience. Engagement is vital for building brand loyalty and understanding your consumers.</p> \n<p>The better you understand them, the better equipped you are to deliver content that resonates.</p> \n<p>The grocery delivery company <a href=\"http://instacart.com\">Instacart</a> hosted its own trivia game on Facebook Stories to test its audience's food knowledge.</p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img alt=\"Instacart Facebook Story Example\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/Examples%20of%20Facebook%20Stories%20for%20Business.gif?width=218&amp;name=Examples%20of%20Facebook%20Stories%20for%20Business.gif\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 218px;\" title=\"\" width=\"218\"></p> \n<p>While this may not necessarily give the brand valuable insight into their audience, their engagement with the post may tell them a lot about the type of content their followers enjoy.</p> \n<p>Want another way to use polls? Tie them to a product or service.</p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Facebook-Story-Example-alaffia.jpg?width=250&amp;name=Facebook-Story-Example-alaffia.jpg\" alt=\"Alaffia Facebook Story Example \" width=\"250\" style=\"width: 250px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\"></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.alaffia.com/\">Alaffia</a> posted a simple poll asking its audience about its product.</p> \n<p>This accomplished two things at once: It introduced followers to a product they may not yet know and it had an interactive element that encouraged audience engagement.</p> \n<h3>User-Generated Content</h3> \n<p>One of the most popular uses for Facebook Stories is user-generated content (UGC). UGC provides what's known as <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/service/psychology-social-proof\">social proof</a>, a psychological phenomenon where we tend to look to others for guidance on what to do.</p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/facebook-story-example-adjourn.jpg?width=250&amp;name=facebook-story-example-adjourn.jpg\" alt=\"Adjourn TeaHouse facebook story example \" width=\"250\" style=\"width: 250px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\"></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.adjournteahouse.com/\">Adjourn Teahouse</a> leverages UGC to show the various ways in which consumers use its products. Because of the Facebook Stories repost feature, the brand can fill its Stories with content already created by others, saving both time and money.</p> \n<p>One thing to note is that because Facebook now owns Instagram, you can repost another user's Instagram content to your Facebook Stories – something that's not available between other social media platforms.</p> \n<p>The brand <a href=\"https://curls.biz/\">Curls</a> uses this same approach to promote its products.</p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img alt=\"Curls Facebook Story Example\" src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Google%20Drive%20Integration/Examples%20of%20Facebook%20Stories%20for%20Business-1.gif?width=234&amp;name=Examples%20of%20Facebook%20Stories%20for%20Business-1.gif\" style=\"margin-left: auto; width: 234px; margin-right: auto; display: block;\" title=\"\" width=\"234\"></p> \n<p>What brand doesn't love free promotion? This type of UGC helps brands gain credibility and earn new customers.</p> \n<h3>Direct to Website Traffic</h3> \n<p>Have an article on your website you want your Facebook followers to read? Take advantage of the \"‘See More\" feature on Facebook Stories. <img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/facebook-stories-example-blavity.jpg?width=250&amp;name=facebook-stories-example-blavity.jpg\" alt=\"Blavity facebook stories example\" width=\"250\" style=\"width: 250px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\"><a href=\"https://blavityinc.com/\">Blavity</a>, a news and media company, often uses this feature to lead Facebook users to its blog posts.</p> \n<p>While this brand mostly directs traffic to its blog posts, businesses can use this feature to lead their followers to landing pages, product pages, or any other webpage.</p> \n<p>What's great about this tool is that it makes it easy for users to navigate to other channels from the brand without ever leaving the Facebook platform.</p> \n<h3>Giveaways</h3> \n<p>If you're<a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/facebook-giveaway\"> hosting a giveaway,</a> you'll likely create a Facebook post so that users can access it beyond the 24-hour window. However, it's important to promote the giveaway on other channels to give it more visibility.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/facebook-stories-example-Blk%26bold.jpg?width=250&amp;name=facebook-stories-example-Blk%26bold.jpg\" alt=\"Blk &amp; Bold facebook stories example\" width=\"250\" style=\"width: 250px; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\">Note how beverage company <a href=\"https://blkandbold.com/\">BLK &amp; Bold</a> promoted its giveaway on Facebook Stories. Instead of posting all of the giveaway details, like the rules and eligibility requirements, the brand highlighted what its audience is most excited most: the giveaway itself.</p> \n<p>If your giveaway is hosted on another social media platform – say Instagram or Twitter – you can still promote it on your Facebook Story and use the \"See More\" feature.</p> \n<p>There's no right or wrong way to post on Facebook Stories. It's all about finding what stories resonate best with your audience.</p> \n<p>Every Story you post is an opportunity to connect with your audience and learn more about them.</p> \n<p>While some of these strategies may not work for your brand, they're worth trying out. Because even stories that don't perform well give you as much insight as those that do.</p> \n<p><a class=\"cta_button\" 01:38:07","updatedTime":"2021-04-08 01:38:07","title":"The Ultimate Guide to Marketing Trends in 2021","link":"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/marketing-trends","description":"<p>Marketing moves at the speed of light … er, at least it feels that way when you’re brainstorming a new campaign or strategy, and all of a sudden, a new statistic or technology release changes <em>everything</em>.</p>  \n<p>On a yearly, quarterly, and even monthly basis, new trends and techniques pop up and transform the way we attract, connect with, and market to our audiences.</p> \n<p>But keeping up with these changes isn’t always enough. To succeed in the fast-paced, marketing world, you have to stay <i>ahead</i> of the game. That’s why we created this guide — influenced by some of our very own HubSpot experts — so you can bookmark and return to some of the most important marketing trends of today, time and time again.</p> \n<p><a class=\"cta_button\" href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/cs/ci/?pg=3d0bc27a-898d-40d5-aa46-8696ed81c4ee&amp;pid=53&amp;ecid=&amp;hseid=&amp;hsic=\"><img class=\"hs-cta-img \" style=\"border-width: 0px; /*hs-extra-styles*/; margin: 0 auto; display: block; margin-top: 20px; margin-bottom: 20px\" alt=\"Download Now: State of Marketing Report [2020 Version]\" src=\"https://no-cache.hubspot.com/cta/default/53/3d0bc27a-898d-40d5-aa46-8696ed81c4ee.png\" align=\"middle\"></a></p> \n<p></p> \n<a></a> \n<h2>Why use marketing trends?</h2> \n<p>If a certain marketing strategy or approach has consistently worked for your business, why change it?</p> \n<p>Well, just because something works now doesn't mean it'll work again in the future. You have to be one step ahead, or at least keep up with the emerging trends, that will impact your marketing success the next time around. So, other than keeping up with developments in the industry, why should your business care about marketing trends?</p> \n<p><strong>Marketing trends allow you to:</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li>Keep up with the way your consumers shop and research your products and services (and those of your competitors')</li> \n <li>Stay up to date with changes in consumer behavior and priorities</li> \n <li>Ensure you're ahead of the curve in terms of knowing who your target audience is and what they need from your business</li> \n <li>Listen and respond to changes in the market to help you save money</li> \n <li>Stay relevant in your target marketplace and among your competitors (now and in the long run)</li> \n</ul> \n<p></p> \n<p>As we've said, many things change in the marketing world — and they do so frequently. That's why we've listed some of the most popular types of marketing trends — and an example or two of each — to help you adapt to these developments as needed and to equip your business with the knowledge necessary for you to succeed.</p> \n<a></a> \n<h3>1. Invest in inbound marketing.</h3> \n<p>This past year, the world dealt with unprecedented change, and outbound marketing tactics became less effective in reaching prospects and leads. The shift from in-person to hybrid work from home (WFH) business practices have made inbound marketing come to the forefront of effective tactics. For example, there’s been a significant rise in virtual events due to COVID-19 forcing marketers to get creative to catch the attention of customers.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/in/johnhazard/\">John Hazard</a>, the founder and content strategist at digital marketing agency Lighthouse Creative Group, sees this as a place of opportunity to generate interest despite their typical formulaic production. “Screen fatigue is a big issue for brands. As virtual events have exploded as a replacement for in-person engagement, every business has tried to roll out ‘events’, webinars, and virtual conferences. But most are just PowerPoint presentations or an executive talking with their kitchen in the background. That’s not interesting … So, the race is on in 2021 for polish and production value — graphics, directors, professional hosts, equipment, and no kitchen backdrops.\"</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/inbound-marketing?_ga=2.137539190.736585117.1617122469-1923623018.1617122469\">Inbound marketing</a> can be a valuable asset to create brand awareness and build trust digitally through refocusing strategy to drive customers to seek out your content.</p> \n<p>The process of <a href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/inbound-marketing?__hstc=233546881.080e9234ed39e55808621ab8e2d9e8e2.1617122470747.1617122470747.1617122470747.1&amp;__hssc=233546881.1.1617122470748&amp;__hsfp=2277871135&amp;_ga=2.137539190.736585117.1617122469-1923623018.1617122469\">inbound marketing</a> requires you to product quality, valuable content tailored towards your target audience and buyer personas and their needs.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://academy.hubspot.com/courses/inbound-marketing?hubs_post-cta=pillar_allphrase&amp;__hstc=233546881.080e9234ed39e55808621ab8e2d9e8e2.1617122470747.1617122470747.1617122470747.1&amp;__hssc=233546881.1.1617122470748&amp;__hsfp=2277871135\"><em>Sign up for a free inbound marketing course to help you begin organically reaching more audience members.</em></a><br><br></p> \n<h3>2. Turn customers into your biggest promoters.</h3> \n<p>The marketing funnel is old news. Today, <a href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/flywheel?__hstc=233546881.080e9234ed39e55808621ab8e2d9e8e2.1617122470747.1617122470747.1617122470747.1&amp;__hssc=233546881.1.1617122470748&amp;__hsfp=2277871135&amp;_ga=2.137539190.736585117.1617122469-1923623018.1617122469\">the flywheel</a> — and a subsequent <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/customers/service-hub\">focus on service</a> — have replaced the one-way direction of the funnel.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Funnel%20vs%20Flywheel.png?width=445&amp;name=Funnel%20vs%20Flywheel.png\" alt=\"Funnel vs Flywheel\" width=\"445\" style=\"width: 445px; display: block; margin: 0px auto;\">In the world of the marketing funnel, customers were an afterthought. Once they became a paying customer, businesses considered them obsolete — until, of course, it was time re-sign that contract.</p> \n<p>The flywheel, on the other hand, places the customer in the center. Since word-of-mouth marketing is one of the most powerful marketing tactics, it’s wise to not only serve your customers but also equip them to become advocates for and promoters of your brand. The flywheel illustrates this process: <strong>excellent service as its own marketing strategy.</strong></p> \n<p><strong>By keeping the flywheel at the center of your marketing efforts, </strong>you'll delight and empower your customers. It’s worthwhile to place a heavy emphasis on customer service and train your team to handle requests and issues.<strong><br></strong></p> \n<p>This will lead to customers who can market <em>for you</em> — they can promote and advocate for your business via their networks both online and in-person.</p> \n<p><strong>Featured Resource</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li><a href=\"https://offers.hubspot.com/case-study-templates?hubs_post-cta=inline-text&amp;__hstc=233546881.080e9234ed39e55808621ab8e2d9e8e2.1617122470747.1617122470747.1617122470747.1&amp;__hssc=233546881.1.1617122470748&amp;__hsfp=2277871135&amp;_ga=2.137539190.736585117.1617122469-1923623018.1617122469\">The Ultimate Customer Case Study Creation Kit (+ Free Templates)</a><br><br></li> \n</ul> \n<a></a> \n<h2>Content Marketing Trends</h2> \n<p>All types of business in a variety of industries are focusing on <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/content-marketing\">content marketing</a> — publishing blogs, investing in resources to produce unique content, and paying for content-related ads.</p> \n<p>So, why should you also care about the current content marketing trends? Because <a href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/marketing-statistics?__hstc=233546881.080e9234ed39e55808621ab8e2d9e8e2.1617122470747.1617122470747.1617122470747.1&amp;__hssc=233546881.1.1617122470748&amp;__hsfp=2277871135&amp;_ga=2.137539190.736585117.1617122469-1923623018.1617122469\">47% of buyers</a> view three to five pieces of content prior to engaging with a sales rep, and the majority of them expect brands to create content to gain their interest.</p> \n<p>To ensure your content marketing efforts are as effective and accessible as possible, pay attention to the type of content that resonates most with your buyer personas, target audience, and current customers.</p> \n<p><strong>Featured Resources</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li><a href=\"https://offers.hubspot.com/content-creation-templates?hubs_post-cta=inline-text&amp;__hstc=233546881.080e9234ed39e55808621ab8e2d9e8e2.1617122470747.1617122470747.1617122470747.1&amp;__hssc=233546881.1.1617122470748&amp;__hsfp=2277871135&amp;_ga=2.137539190.736585117.1617122469-1923623018.1617122469\">386+ Content Creation Templates</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"https://offers.hubspot.com/blog-post-templates?hubs_post-cta=inline-text&amp;__hstc=233546881.080e9234ed39e55808621ab8e2d9e8e2.1617122470747.1617122470747.1617122470747.1&amp;__hssc=233546881.1.1617122470748&amp;__hsfp=2277871135&amp;_ga=2.137539190.736585117.1617122469-1923623018.1617122469\">5 Free Blog Post Templates</a><br><br></li> \n</ul> \n<h3>3. Create and share video content.</h3> \n<p><a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/video-marketing\">Video marketing</a> isn’t a new idea, but its effectiveness and popularity have definitely skyrocketed in recent years, and even more with the onset of the pandemic.</p> \n<p>HubSpot Senior Copywriter and Brand Campaigns Manager <a href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/in/aliciacollins/\">Alicia Collins</a> and Senior Motion Designer <a href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/in/conleymn/\">Megan Conley</a>, weigh in: “This [consumer behavior] also indicates that video can be used throughout all parts of the flywheel — not just as an asset for marketing. When incorporating video, businesses have historically used it as a means of introducing their brand and product or service offerings. But that’s not the case anymore. Video can be a valuable addition to both sales and customer service efforts.”</p> \n<p>In the past, video was limited due to costly resources and production. Today, it’s much more accessible. With a lower-cost barrier, video has become less intimidating to incorporate into your marketing efforts.</p> \n<p>You don’t have to hire a production team or marketing agency; all you need is a smartphone, such as an iPhone, and an editing software, such as <a href=\"https://www.adobe.com/products/premiere.html\">Adobe Premiere Pro</a>.</p> \n<p><strong>Featured Resources</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li><a href=\"https://offers.hubspot.com/beginners-guide-to-video-marketing?hubs_post-cta=inline-text\">The Ultimate Video Marketing Starter Pack</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"https://offers.hubspot.com/youtube-for-business?hubs_post-cta=inline-text\">YouTube for Business: A 30-Day Roadmap for Channel Growth</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"https://offers.hubspot.com/video-in-each-stage-of-the-buyers-journey?hubs_post-cta=inline-text\">How to Use Video in Every Stage of the Buyer's Journey</a><br><br></li> \n</ul> \n<h3>4. Reach new audiences with native advertising.</h3> \n<p>When your brand pays to feature content on a third-party website, you’re investing in <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/native-advertising-what-you-need-to-know\">native advertising</a>. Unlike traditional advertising, which is designed to interrupt and stand out, native advertising is designed to blend in and promote your brand to a new audience who might otherwise never learn about you.</p> \n<p>Because native ads don’t “feel” like traditional ads, consumers are more likely to consume them — in fact, consumers view native ads over <a href=\"https://www.sharethrough.com/resources/in-feed-ads-vs-banner-ads/\">50% more</a> than banner ads. <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/native-advertising-examples\">Examples of native advertising</a> can be found on social media, through search engine results, content recommendation platforms (those links to various other content you can click at the bottom of the page to read more on or related to the topic), or in campaigns.</p> \n<p>For example, <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/\">Instagram</a> is a popular social media network that routinely partners with brands for native advertising. By taking advantage of the Instagram Story or Shop features, brands are able to share posts that look similar to the average user’s followers posting style, while subtly advertising a product.<img src=\"https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/IrC4OdtMmbZyv7SAvoeTbn-u1oU_HuX1_ymOcpLyKoDx3o4-57SAD5NFR8oN0vIXO3V9AT859gZAMDxZr6TAziNk0K46aB1mMfHRBdNQf0NpRujrcg17Lr7iEJkNRJU464amnNHH\" width=\"624\" height=\"324\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\" alt=\"instagram native advertising for makeup on iphone\"></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center; font-size: 13px;\"><a href=\"https://taplink.at/en/blog/native_advertising_what_it_is_examples_of_native_advertising_on_instagram.html\"><em>Source</em></a></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: left;\">To incorporate native advertising in your marketing efforts, look for publications relevant to your brand. Remember to sound natural and avoid coming off as pushy or blatantly promotional.</p> \n<a></a> \n<h2>Social Media Marketing Trends</h2> In the U.S. alone, \n<a href=\"https://www.statista.com/statistics/273476/percentage-of-us-population-with-a-social-network-profile/\" style=\"font-size: 1rem;\">79% of people</a> have some type of social media account — and globally, there are over 3.7 billion social media users. \n<p>This is why social media marketing is a popular channel that's become a part of almost every business’s greater marketing strategy. Social media marketing allows you to authentically connect with your audience on a personal level, humanizing your brand.</p> \n<p><strong>Featured Resources</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li><a href=\"https://offers.hubspot.com/how-to-use-twitter-for-business?hubs_post-cta=inline-text&amp;__hstc=233546881.080e9234ed39e55808621ab8e2d9e8e2.1617122470747.1617122470747.1617122470747.1&amp;__hssc=233546881.1.1617122470748&amp;__hsfp=2277871135&amp;_ga=2.196199530.736585117.1617122469-1923623018.1617122469\">How to Use Twitter for Business (+ Follower Growth Tracking Template)</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"https://offers.hubspot.com/30-days-of-instagram?hubs_post-cta=inline-text&amp;__hstc=233546881.080e9234ed39e55808621ab8e2d9e8e2.1617122470747.1617122470747.1617122470747.1&amp;__hssc=233546881.1.1617122470748&amp;__hsfp=2277871135&amp;_ga=2.196199530.736585117.1617122469-1923623018.1617122469\">30 Days of Instagram: A Guide for Businesses</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"https://offers.hubspot.com/how-to-attract-customers-with-facebook?hubs_post-cta=inline-text&amp;__hstc=233546881.080e9234ed39e55808621ab8e2d9e8e2.1617122470747.1617122470747.1617122470747.1&amp;__hssc=233546881.1.1617122470748&amp;__hsfp=2277871135&amp;_ga=2.196199530.736585117.1617122469-1923623018.1617122469\">How to Attract Customers With Facebook</a><br><br></li> \n</ul> \n<h3>5. Be Transparent with Diversity and Inclusion.</h3> \n<p>As the Coronavirus pandemic took its toll on the world, it highlighted the pains that employees had to endure in the workplace and in politics. Employees became more vocal about their frustrations about feeling unequal as members of society and in their treatment in office.</p> \n<p>Companies are now moving their social media strategies to include more diversity and inclusion initiatives, and it’s a good marketing move as well. The Senior Lecturer in Leadership and Innovation, <a href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/in/halgregersen/\">Hal Gregersen</a>, shares his perspective on the subject:</p> \n<p>“If there can be a perfect storm of opportunity for strengthening D&amp;I [diversity and inclusion] in organizations, I believe it is happening now. I saw public and private conversations about diversity, equity, and fairness reach new heights during 2020, which will likely cause barriers to change or fade. With the pandemic, traditional ways of doing business and of working were upended, and now, barriers to the idea of change are dissolving.”</p> \n<p>Companies that are trying to change with the times should become more transparent about their efforts to make the workplace more equal and their plans to expand their diversity and inclusion initiatives.</p> \n<h3>6. Leverage both ephemeral and permanent social media content.</h3> \n<p>Not all social media is created equal. Different types of content do better on various platforms. This includes ephemeral (fleeting) and permanent (long-lasting) social media content. Let's take a deeper look at ephemeral vs. permanent social content:</p> \n<h4><strong>Ephemeral Social Media Marketing</strong></h4> \n<p>Today, Instagram and Facebook Stories specifically make the creation of ephemeral content simple — Instagram and Facebook Stories are photos and videos that live for 24-hours before disappearing “forever”. (Well, not really … there’s an Archive feature where all your Stories reside after they expire. But you get the gist.)</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/in/kellyhendricksondesign/\">Kelly Hendrickson</a>, a social media marketing manager at HubSpot, says: “Ephemeral content versus permanent content is often dictated by the social platform, as well as by the audience's behavior on the platform.”</p> \n<p>Take Instagram, for example:</p> \n<p>“[Instagram] Stories are soaring in popularity, and the user behavior on Stories leans toward playful, low-fi, quick content with heavy use of features within the UX (gifs, boomerangs, polls, etc). Their fleeting design isn’t the only differentiating factor. Instagram Stories can be heavily edited, too, with filters, GIFs, colored text, and more. Because of these fun additions, brands have added a brand new strategy for producing and publishing ephemeral content that varies from their other social media content.”</p> \n<h4><strong>Permanent Social Media Content</strong></h4> \n<p>Permanent content is a little different:</p> \n<p>“Instagram can organically serve up a wall post across a wide span of time, so there's less of an opportunity for brands to be timely (who wants to see New Year's post when they’ve already given up on their resolutions?!). Since Instagram users are more <a href=\"https://sproutsocial.com/insights/instagram-stats/\">active on weekdays</a>, during the standard workday, it seems users are looking for a break!</p> \n<p>It’s critical to use your brand voice and point of view to find how you can serve your audience during that break. Should your presence be inspirational, beautiful, informative, playful, or trendy? They all have a place on Instagram’s permanent wall, it just needs to match your brand’s message.”</p> \n<p>By combining ephemeral and permanent social media content on platforms such as Instagram and Facebook, you allow your business to showcase more of your brand’s personality and flair.</p> \n<p>Hendrickson says, “The combo of a running clock and a lively audience is a huge opportunity for brands to lean into quick, in-the-moment content that showcases the more light-hearted elements of their brand. Succinctness and clarity are key in content.”</p> \n<p><strong>Featured Resource</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li><a href=\"https://offers.hubspot.com/instagram-stories-for-small-business?hubs_post-cta=inline-text&amp;__hstc=233546881.080e9234ed39e55808621ab8e2d9e8e2.1617122470747.1617122470747.1617122470747.1&amp;__hssc=233546881.1.1617122470748&amp;__hsfp=2277871135&amp;_ga=2.196199530.736585117.1617122469-1923623018.1617122469\">Instagram Stories for Business: 6 Tips from the Pros</a><br><br></li> \n</ul> \n<h3>7. Work with micro-influencers.</h3> \n<p><a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/how-to-work-with-influencers\">Influencer marketing</a> plays a major role in all types of modern marketing (ads, videos, social media, blogs). But businesses are no longer limited to major celebrities and names that <em>everyone</em> knows when deciding to work with an influencer.</p> \n<p>In fact, <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/micro-influencer-marketing\">micro-influencers</a> have found their niche in the social media world, too — and it's a big role they've started to play in converting leads, connecting with audience members, and boosting brand awareness.</p> \n<p>Micro-influencers are social media promoters with a smaller, niche following (typically, thousands to tens-of-thousands of followers). Although these folks may have fewer followers, their posts often pack more punch due to their higher level of engagement.</p> \n<p>Additionally, since they’re considered “average” and “everyday” people (unlike hard-to-reach celebrities), audience members view micro-influencers more like friends and family and, therefore, are <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/how-to-work-with-influencers?_ga=2.95753756.1692201945.1563204441-527251855.1560789477\">more likely to trust their opinions and recommendations</a>.</p> \n<p>Rosie, known as The Londoner, is a popular travel and lifestyle influencer on Instagram. She has over 330k loyal followers who interact and engage with her posts. The below image of a post on profile shows that with almost 36,000 likes, Rosie is garnering almost 11% engagement.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Screen%20Shot%202018-08-03%20at%2012.47.05%20PM.png?width=1500&amp;name=Screen%20Shot%202018-08-03%20at%2012.47.05%20PM.png\" alt=\"social media marketing trend micro influencer\" width=\"1500\" style=\"width: 1500px; display: block; margin: 0px auto;\"></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center; font-size: 13px;\"><a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/rosielondoner/\"><em>Source</em></a></p> \n<p>Micro-influencers are the future of influencer marketing. Although it may be tempting to only look at the number of followers a user has to determine their influence, remember <strong>true influence lives in engagement rates </strong>(clicks, subscribes, and purchases).</p> \n<p>They also drive social buzz through the creation and posting of personal content and are much more cost-effective for your business.</p> \n<p><strong>Featured Resources</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li><a href=\"https://offers.hubspot.com/how-to-become-an-influencer-in-your-industry-free-ebook?hubs_post-cta=inline-text&amp;__hstc=233546881.080e9234ed39e55808621ab8e2d9e8e2.1617122470747.1617122470747.1617122470747.1&amp;__hssc=233546881.1.1617122470748&amp;__hsfp=2277871135&amp;_ga=2.125035212.736585117.1617122469-1923623018.1617122469\">How to Become an Influencer in Your Industry</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"https://offers.hubspot.com/6-step-process-maximise-influencer-marketing?hubs_post-cta=inline-text&amp;__hstc=233546881.080e9234ed39e55808621ab8e2d9e8e2.1617122470747.1617122470747.1617122470747.1&amp;__hssc=233546881.1.1617122470748&amp;__hsfp=2277871135&amp;_ga=2.125035212.736585117.1617122469-1923623018.1617122469\">The 6-Step Process to Maximize Your Influencer Outreach</a><br><br></li> \n</ul> \n<a></a> \n<h2>Search Engine Optimization Marketing Trends</h2> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/marketing-statistics?__hstc=233546881.080e9234ed39e55808621ab8e2d9e8e2.1617122470747.1617122470747.1617122470747.1&amp;__hssc=233546881.1.1617122470748&amp;__hsfp=2277871135&amp;_ga=2.125035212.736585117.1617122469-1923623018.1617122469\" style=\"font-size: 1rem;\">61% of marketers</a> say improving search engine optimization (SEO) to grow their organic presence online is their top inbound marketing priority.</p> \n<p>Are you one of these marketers? If so, have you figured out how exactly you plan to improve your SEO and organic presence? When you optimize for specific types of consumer behavior, you'll help your business become more discoverable online.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://offers.hubspot.com/seo-starter-pack?hubs_post-cta=pillar-header?hubs_post-cta=pillar_allphrase&amp;__hstc=233546881.080e9234ed39e55808621ab8e2d9e8e2.1617122470747.1617122470747.1617122470747.1&amp;__hssc=233546881.1.1617122470748&amp;__hsfp=2277871135&amp;_ga=2.125035212.736585117.1617122469-1923623018.1617122469\"><em>Download a free SEO Starter Kit to get your website and content ranking in search in 2019.</em></a></p> \n<h3>8. Repurposing content across channels.</h3> \n<p>This marketing trend is going to be a much bigger focus for many marketers this year. Companies that already have poured their energy into creating high-quality content should be making it more accessible on different platforms, and more up to date.</p> \n<p>Instead of coming up with new ideas, marketers are going to be taking what’s worked in the past and optimizing it for the present.</p> \n<p>In SEO, keeping your content up to date and full of rich, engaging content will outweigh older work that is lacking in keyword relevancy with old statistics and links. Not only that, but taking existing content and repurposing it for a new podcast, webinar, or blog post can be an efficient way to keep it relevant in search engines.</p> \n<h3>9. Implement voice search tactics.</h3> \n<p>It's probably safe to assume you’ve used Siri, Alexa, Cortana, and/ or Google Assistant in the last month or so. Am I right?</p> \n<p>Not only do these digital assistants answer short, informational queries such as “<em>Who is the actor in Mission: Impossible?</em>” or “<em>What’s the weather in Boston today?</em>”, but they’ve also started to process more local, conversational, and customized searches. These may sound like, “<em>Where’s a nearby coffee shop I can work from today?</em>”, “<em>How late is it open?</em>”, and “<em>Do they serve iced coffee?</em>”</p> \n<p>Because of this emerging behavior, businesses need to respond and change the way they frame information. Instead of catering to Google’s manual search algorithm, <strong>optimize your content by</strong> <strong>framing it around questions</strong>.</p> \n<p>When you implement voice search tactics this way, you'll empower your users to get the answers they want and need. They can ask a question in that conversational tone we mentioned above and, in return, they'll get a high-quality and accurate response. They can multitask while asking questions and receiving answers, as well as get those answers they're looking for more quickly.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/in/ajafrost/\">Aja Frost</a>, Head of English SEO at HubSpot, says: “Businesses should look at a topic and say, ‘<em>What questions could users ask about this?</em>’ Then, they should plan sub-topics accordingly and look for opportunities to insert questions as headers. This will allow voice assistants to easily grab questions and recognize content as solutions.”</p> \n<p>Frost also encourages businesses to look for <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/news-trends/winning-googles-featured-snippet\">featured snippet</a> opportunities, which are the information previews Google provides when users search for definitions or questions. Voice assistants typically pull responses directly from these boxes.</p> \n<p><strong>Featured Resource</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li><a href=\"https://offers.hubspot.com/how-to-conduct-technical-seo-audit?hubs_post-cta=inline-text\">How to Conduct a Technical SEO Audit</a></li> \n <li><a href=\"https://offers.hubspot.com/seo-myths?hubs_post-cta=inline-text&amp;_ga=2.257608067.966330271.1565107559-1493293515.1553017609\">22 SEO Myths to Leave Behind in 2019</a><br><br></li> \n</ul> \n<h3>10. Offer a responsive, mobile-friendly website design.</h3> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/marketing-statistics?_ga=2.17698097.966330271.1565107559-1493293515.1553017609\">48% of consumers</a> start mobile research with a search engine, and the first position on Google search results on mobile has a 31.35% click-through rate.</p> \n<p>It goes without saying that mobile usage is skyrocketing, especially for search queries and research. Due to this, businesses should ensure their website is discoverable and <i>readable</i> via mobile devices including smartphones and tablets. Website speed is also becoming important as Google prioritizes better performing websites in their search engine results pages (SERPs).</p> \n<p>Become familiar with how to <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/mobile-website-design-examples\">design and optimize your website for mobile use</a>. This typically requires a <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/responsive-web-design\">responsive design</a> — meaning your website will “respond” and change its design and layout as users access it on their desktop versus their smartphone.</p> \n<p><strong>Featured Resource</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li><a href=\"https://offers.hubspot.com/marketers-guide-to-mobile?hubs_post-cta=inline-text&amp;_ga=2.257608067.966330271.1565107559-1493293515.1553017609\">The Marketer's Guide to Mobile</a><br><br></li> \n</ul> \n<a></a> \n<h2>Technology Marketing Trends</h2> \n<p>Similar to marketing, technology is also ever-changing — and it's happening equally as fast (if not faster). There are a number of ways to use technology to your advantage when it comes to your marketing, especially since so many new opportunities are emerging every day.<br><br></p> \n<h3>11. Improving content experience.</h3> \n<p>Clicking onto a landing page plagued in slow pop-ups, advertisements, and cluttered formatting is an easy way to convince readers to leave it. While your company’s product or service should be a main focus, the way you present it should be just as important.</p> \n<p>If customers have a hard time navigating your website, it will be more frustrating to continue digging through it than to look elsewhere for content.</p> \n<p>Clear web pages with visually interesting segments will give your company the chance to attract prospects. For example, web design company Lounge Lizard shows the future of a stunning, interactive, quick loading home page.</p> \n<p><img src=\"https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/jl0nf4KFV3T7a-Ig97kOdi68NXqqnojHYpuOIE3znN3z50uaaSqoRCvI8cYjR17OMcl3WgZn8bQ1bP7-4EJZmOAzblAH6ykD7H2Ge2ISNvOnZwX53hNVqDmVnRWE7zNDe4TKNypz\" width=\"624\" height=\"383\" alt=\"lounge lizard interactive fast loading home page\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block;\"></p> \n<p style=\"text-align: center; font-size: 13px;\"><a href=\"https://www.loungelizard.com/\"><em>Source</em></a></p> \n<p>Implementing interactive content and better UX and UI design for a website is a marketing trend that will never become obsolete.</p> \n<h3>12. Integrate artificial intelligence (AI).</h3> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/stories/artificial-intelligence?__hstc=233546881.080e9234ed39e55808621ab8e2d9e8e2.1617122470747.1617122470747.1617122470747.1&amp;__hssc=233546881.1.1617122470748&amp;__hsfp=2277871135&amp;_ga=2.201059688.736585117.1617122469-1923623018.1617122469\">Artificial intelligence</a> refers to a subset of computer science that teaches machines to do things that would require intelligence if done by a human. Think of tasks like learning, seeing, talking, socializing, reasoning, or problem-solving. When completed by computers, they’re considered AI.</p> \n<p>AI has completely infiltrated our daily lives and tasks. When Spotify recommends a song, Facebook recognizes and tags a person, or you text a friend using Siri, you’re tapping into AI. As we utilize AI more and more (especially as consumers), marketers and businesses will need to respond.</p> \n<p>The point of AI isn’t to replace humans or the need for a human touch. It’s to improve and expand our ability to connect with our audience and help them solve their problems quicker and more thoroughly.</p> \n<p>In fact, authenticity in marketing is <a href=\"https://www.elegantthemes.com/blog/marketing/authenticity-in-marketing-why-does-it-matter\">more important than ever</a> to consumers. AI is also incredibly helpful when collecting and analyzing data and making data-driven decisions. So, research ways you can incorporate AI into your business's marketing strategies to better serve your consumers and to make your life simpler.</p> \n<h3>13. Use virtual reality (VR) &amp; augmented reality (AR).</h3> \n<p><a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/virtual-reality-vr\">Virtual reality</a> is viewing a computer-generated, lifelike scenario. <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/augmented-reality-ar\">Augmented reality</a> is viewing the real world augmented with visual, haptic, olfactory or visual additions. VR and AR offer different experiences, but both are making waves in the marketing world today.</p> \n<p>They’re affecting your lives, too. Ever watched a 360° video on Facebook? That’s VR. What about IKEA’s <a href=\"https://itunes.apple.com/us/app/ikea-place/id1279244498?mt=8\">IKEA PLACE app</a> which helps you visualize virtual furniture in your very real room? That’s AR.</p> \n<div class=\"hs-responsive-embed-wrapper hs-responsive-embed\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 100%; height: auto; position: relative; overflow: hidden; min-width: 256px; margin: 0px auto; padding: 0;\"> \n <div class=\"hs-responsive-embed-inner-wrapper\" style=\"position: relative; overflow: hidden; max-width: 100%; padding-bottom: 56.07%; margin: 0;\">\n  <iframe class=\"hs-responsive-embed-target-iframe hs-fullwidth-embed hs-responsive-embed-iframe\" style=\"position: absolute; top: 0; left: 0; width: 100%; height: 100%; border: none;\" src=\"http://www.youtube.com/embed/r0ViFTEb8aQ\" width=\"560\" height=\"314\" allowfullscreen></iframe>\n </div> \n</div> \n<p>VR and AR are used to supplement and improve customer experiences online and at events. Generally speaking, this is a trend marketers have been slower to adopt due to pricey equipment and bulky headsets. But, as VR glasses and AR apps become more accessible, businesses can expect to add this technology to their marketing strategy.<br><br></p> \n<h3><strong>14. Include chatbots on your site. </strong></h3> \n<p>Did you know that more than half of consumers expect a response <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/news-trends/live-chat-go-to-market-flaw\">within 10 minutes</a> to any marketing, sales, or customer service inquiry? How can this be humanly possible?</p> \n<p>It’s not … for humans, anyway. Enter: <a href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/stories/chatbot-marketing-future\">Chatbots</a>.</p> \n<p>Bots are powered by a computer program that automates certain tasks, typically by chatting with a user through a conversational interface. Bots are made possible by artificial intelligence which helps it understand complex requests, personalize responses, and improve interactions over time.</p> \n<p>Bots provide quick, easy solutions to problems of all levels of complexity. No longer is the need for live chat or a literal one-to-one digital conversation. Bots provide the perception and dedication of a 1:1 service experience while working with hundreds of customers — something that no customer service representative or team would ever be able to do.</p> \n<p>To the consumers who hate repeating themselves to multiple sales or service representatives (<a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/news-trends/live-chat-go-to-market-flaw\">33%, to be exact</a>), listen up — chatbots are and will continue making your lives <i style=\"color: inherit; font-size: 1.1rem;\">much</i> easier. If used correctly, they manage conversations at scale and aggregate data from multiple sources of data, from calendars to knowledge bases to blog posts and videos.</p> \n<div class=\"hs-responsive-embed-wrapper hs-responsive-embed\" style=\"margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; display: block; width: 100%; height: auto; position: relative; overflow: hidden; min-width: 256px; margin: 0px auto; padding: 0;\"> \n <div class=\"hs-responsive-embed-inner-wrapper\" style=\"position: relative; overflow: hidden; max-width: 100%; padding-bottom: 56.07%; margin: 0;\">\n  <iframe class=\"hs-responsive-embed-target-iframe hs-fullwidth-embed hs-responsive-embed-iframe\" style=\"position: absolute; top: 0; left: 0; width: 100%; height: 100%; border: none;\" src=\"http://www.youtube.com/embed/wL7-PoiBiKM\" width=\"560\" height=\"314\" allowfullscreen></iframe>\n </div> \n</div> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.linkedin.com/in/jondick/\">Jon Dick</a>, SVP of Marketing at HubSpot, says: “It’s on you to make things as easy as possible. Your buyers want to use live chat? You should give it to them. They’ve had the same problem three times in the last month? You should already know, and have a plan to fix it.”</p> \n<p><strong>Featured Resource</strong></p> \n<ul> \n <li><a href=\"https://offers.hubspot.com/stay-current-emerging-tech?hubs_post-cta=inline-text\">How to Stay Current on Emerging Technology Trends</a><br><br></li> \n</ul> \n<a></a> \n<h2>Privacy Marketing Trends</h2> \n<p>In the marketing world, data is highly valuable … and not just valuable to <i>you</i>, as a marketer or business owner. Whether it's an email address, credit card information, or smartphone location, consumers also view their data as precious and privileged — and it’s your responsibility to take care of it.<br><br></p> \n<h3>15. Give your customers greater control over their data.</h3> \n<p>Whether a software company, bank, government agency, or lemonade stand, every business operates using data. It’s the lifeblood of all things marketing, sales, service, and more.</p> \n<p>And hackers know it. When data breaches happen, precious information is siphoned into the wrong hands, leading to untrustworthy businesses and exploited consumers.</p> \n<p>That’s why the <a href=\"https://blog.hubspot.com/marketing/general-data-protection-regulation-consumer-attitudes\">General Data Protection Regulation</a> (GDPR) was enacted — it's an effort by the EU to give greater control to consumers over their data. Under the GDPR, organizations must ensure that their data is collected legally and safely and that those who collect and manage said data will protect it and respect consumers’ rights.</p> \n<p>Following the GDPR guidelines might seem like a burden, but being fined for non-compliance will feel much heavier; fines range from 10 million euros to 4% of a company's annual global revenue.</p> \n<p>Is this a risk you want to take?</p> \n<p>Probably not — so, do your research. <a href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/data-privacy/gdpr?_ga=2.55356707.966330271.1565107559-1493293515.1553017609\">Learn about GDPR</a> and peruse our <a href=\"https://www.hubspot.com/data-privacy/gdpr-checklist?_ga=2.18549425.966330271.1565107559-1493293515.1553017609\">GDPR checklist</a> to ensure your business is compliant.<br><br></p> \n<h2>Use Marketing Trends to Grow Better</h2> \n<p>You’re up to speed … for now. If your current campaigns and advertising don’t align with these trends, don’t fret. Slowly apply these changes to your marketing efforts and ensure all of your activities are compliant and legal.</p> \n<p>As long as you’re keeping a thumb on the pulse of current marketing trends — and always remain open to change — your business won't fall behind.</p> \n<p><em>Editor's note: This post was originally published in August 2019 and has been updated for comprehensiveness.</em></p>
